The `public contributions` by users in Indonesia on `2023/2/4 4:29 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Indonesia` and cities `Jakarta` `Bandung` `Surabaya` `Makassar` `Medan` `Semarang` `Palembang` `Depok`.

There are `1 countries` and `8 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/lintangtimur/top-github-users).

There are `1927 users`  in Indonesia. You need at least `59 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
